<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kindness is the sunshine of social life.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>仁慈是社会生活中的阳光。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kindness will creep where it may not go.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>仁慈可进入任何禁地。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kind words are the music of the world.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>善言是世上的音乐。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kind words are worth much and cost little.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>口头方便不费力。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kind words butter no parsnips.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>画饼充饥。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Kinsman helps kinsman, but woe to him that hath nothing.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>亲帮亲，邻帮邻，无亲无助你倒霉。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knavery may serve, but honestyis best.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>欺诈可能得计，但诚实总是上策。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge advances by steps not by leaps.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识的获得是循序渐进而不是突飞猛进的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge comes from experience alone.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识来自经验。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is a comfortable and necessary retreat and shelter for us in an advanced age; and if we do not plant it when young, it will give us no shade when we grow old.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>学识可使老年时舒适地退隐和有所寄托；但如果年青时不使它扎下根，老年就得不到它的庇护。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is a treasure, but practice is the key to it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识是一座宝库，实践是打开宝库的钥匙。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is long, life is short.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>吾生有涯，而知无涯。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is of two kinds, we know a subject ourselves, or we know where we can find information upon it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识有两种，一种是我们自己知道的东西，另一种是知道哪里可以找到有关的资料。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is power.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识就是力量。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is the antidote to fear.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识可以解除恐惧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge is the most precious treasure of all things, because it can never be given away, nor stolen nor consumed.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识是万物中最珍贵的财宝，丢不掉，偷不走，也不会损耗。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge makes humble; ignorance makes proud.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识令人谦虚；无知使人骄傲。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge will not be aquired without pain and application.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不花力气，不下功夫是得不到知识的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Knowledge without practice makes but half an artist.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>只有知识而无实践，只能造就半瓢水的艺术家。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Know something like the palm of one's hand.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>熟知其事，了如指掌。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Know something of everything and everything of something.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>既要有一般常识，又要有专业知识。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Know thyself.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知道你自己。  </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Labour is light where love doth pay.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>爱情作酬报，劳苦必轻松。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Labour is often the father of pleasure.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>勤劳常为快乐之源。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Labour is the capital of our working men.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>劳动力是劳动人民的资本。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lack of knowledge is darker than night.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>没有知识比黑夜还要黑。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Late repentance is seldom true.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>后悔少有诚意。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Laugh and grow fat.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>心宽体胖。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Laugh, and the world laughs with you; weep, and you weep alone.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>你笑，人人陪你笑；你哭，惟独你自哭。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Laugh at your ills, And save doctors' bills.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生病不忧虑，节省医药费。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Laugh before breakfast you'll cry before supper.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>乐极生悲。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Law makers should not be law breakers.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>正人先正己。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Laws catch flies but let hornets go free.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>法网只捉苍蝇，不捉黄蜂。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lawsuits consume time, and money, and rest, and friends.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>诉讼将消耗时间、金钱、休息和失去朋友。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lazy folks take the most pains.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>懒汉多吃苦。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learning is an ornament in prosperity, a refuge in adversity, and a provision in old age.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>学问在得意时是装饰品，失意时是庇护所，年老时是供应品。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learning is wealth to the poor, an honour to the rich, an aid to the young, and a support and comfort to the aged.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>学问是穷人的财富，是富人的荣誉，是青年的帮助，是老年的支持和安慰。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learning makes a good man better and ill man worse.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识能使好人更好，坏人更坏。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learning without thought is labour lost; thought without learning is perilous.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>学而不思则罔，思而不学则殆。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn to creep before you leap.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>循序渐进。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn to say before you sing.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>按部就班。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn to suffer without complaining; that is the best thing I can teach you.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>要学会受痛苦而不怨，这是我教你的至要之事。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn to walk before you run.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>循序渐进。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn wisdom by the follies of others.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>要从别人的愚行中学到聪明。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Learn young, learn fair.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>学习趁年轻，既学就学好。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Least said, soonest mended.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>多说反坏事。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lend your money and lose your friend.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>赔了夫人又折兵。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let beggars match with beggars.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>龙配龙，凤配凤。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let bygones be bygones.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>既往不昝。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let difficulties occur but not the loss of courage.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>纵使困难重重，也不丧失勇气。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let every man praise the bridge he goes over.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>饮水思源。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let every man speak well of the bridge theat carries him over.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>饮水思源。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let every tub stand on its own bottom.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>各人管各人自己。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let not the cobbler go beyond his last.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>安分守己。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let not the sun go down upon thy wrath.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>日落之前，平息你的怒火吧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let our object be our courtry, our whole country, and nothing but our country.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们的心目中要有国家，要有整个国家，而且只有我们的国家别如其他。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let's cross the bridge when we come to it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>既来之，则安之。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let sleeping dogs lie.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不要惹事生非。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let the cobbler stick to his last.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>安分守己。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let the dead bury the dead.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>往事不重提。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let the hands get busy, not the mouth.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>手要勤劳，嘴莫多说。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let things take their course.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>听其自然。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Let your yea be yea and your nay be nay.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>是就是，非就非。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Liars have need of good memories.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>谎言者要有好的记忆力。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Liars should have good memories.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>说谎的人应有好的记性。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Liberty consists in the power of doing that which is permitted by law.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>自由就是做法律许可做的事情的权力。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Liberty is not licence.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>自由不是放纵。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Liberty often degenerates into lawlessness.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>自由随便，经常堕落到无法无天。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lie in (oron) the bed one has made.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>自作自受。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lies have short legs.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>谎言是站不住脚的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life if made up of little things.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生活是由琐事构成的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is a battle from cradle to grave.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生是一场从生到死的战斗。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is a comedy to him who thinks and a tragedy to him who feels.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>对善思考者，人生为喜剧；对凭感觉者，人生为悲剧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is a flower of which love is the honey.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生是花朵，爱情是花蜜。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is a shuttle 生活犹如梭子。 </font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center></center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is but a span.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生如朝露。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is compared to voyage.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生好比是航海。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is half spent before we know what it is.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>等到认识人生，已经一半过去了。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is long if you know how to use it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如果懂得好好利用，生命就长了。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is measured by thought and action, not by time.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生命的价值是用思想和行为来衡量的，而不是寿命的长短。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is not all beer and skittles.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生并不全是吃喝玩乐。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is not so short but there is time enougn for courtesy.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生虽短，但表示礼貌的时间还是足够的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is short and time is fleeting 人生短暂，光阴易逝。 </font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center></center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life is sweet.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生命是甜美的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life, to be worthy of a rational being, must be always in progression.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人生必须永远前进，才不愧为有理智的人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Life without a friend is death without a witness.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>在世无朋友，死后无证人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lightly come, lightly go.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>易得易失。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Light troubles speak; great troubles are silent.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>小困难，大声叫嚷；大困难，闷生不响。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like attracts like.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>物以类聚。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like author, like book.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>书如其人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like begets like.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有其父必有其子。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like cow, like calf.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有其父必有其子。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like cures like.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>以毒攻毒。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like draws to like.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>物以类聚。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like draws to like the whole world over.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>物以类聚，世间皆如此。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like father, like son.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有其父必有其子。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like knows like.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>英雄识英雄。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Like tree, like fruit.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有其因必有其果。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Little boats must keep the shores.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>小船不能航行远。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Little bodies may have great souls.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>小小的躯体会有伟大的心灵。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Little thieves are hanged, but great one's escape.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>窃钩者诛，窃国者侯。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Little things amuse little minds.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>小人志卑。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Little wealth, little care.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>财少寡忧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Live and learn.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>活到老，学到老。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Live and let live.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>自己生活，也要让他人生活。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Live to learn and learn to live.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生而学之，学而生之。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Living without an aim is like sailing without a compass.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>生活没有目标，犹如航海没有罗盘。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lock the stable door before the steed is stolen.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>马未偷走前，厩门先锁上。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Loftiest trees most dread the thunder.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>树大招风。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Look before you leap; see before you go.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>三思而行。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lose not time; be always employed in something useful; cut off all unnecessary actions.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不要浪费时间，做些有益的事情，停止一切不必要的行动。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Losers are always in the wrong.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>失败者总是错的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Losses make us more cautious 损失使人更谨慎。 </font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center></center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lost time is never found again, and what we call time enough always proves little enough.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>时间一去不再来，我们常说时间充足，实际。总是不够。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Lost wealth can be replaced by industry, lost knowledge by study, lost health by temperance or medicine, but lost time is gone for ever.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>失去的财富可由勤奋而恢复，失去的知识可由学习而恢复，失去的健康可由节制或药物而恢复，但失去的时间却一去永不复返。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Love all, trust a few, be false to none.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>要爱一切人，相信少数人，不要负于任何人。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our best friends are they who tell us our faults and help us to mend them.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>最好的朋友是指出我们的缺点并帮助改正的人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our bravest and best lessons are not learnt through success, but through misadventure.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>最美好的教训不是得之于成功，而是来之于不幸。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our greatest glory consists not in never falling, but in rising every time we fall.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们最大的光荣并不在于永不跌倒，而在于每次跌倒后能起来。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our happiness consists not in killing others, but in sacrificing ourselves for others.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们最大幸福并不是杀害别人，而是为别人而牺牲自己。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our own actions are our security, not others' judgements.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们的行为是自己的保证而不是别人的鉴定。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Our sweetest songs are those that tell of saddest thought.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>最甜美的的歌是诉说最悲伤的哀思。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Out of debt, out of danger.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>无债一身轻。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Out of sight, out of mind.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>久违情疏。眼不见，心不烦？ </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Overdone is worse than undone.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>过犹不及。  </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Pain is forgotten where gain follows.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>好了伤疤忘了痛。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Pardoning the bad is injuring the good.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>饶了坏人便伤了好人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience and application will carry us through.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐和努力会使我们度过难关。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience is a flower that grows not in everyone's garden.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐是朵花，并非人人园中都开发。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience is a plaster for all sores.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐是治疗一切伤痛的药膏。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience is a virtue.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐是一种美德。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience is bitter, but its fruit is sweet.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐是苦痛的，但它的果实是甜蜜的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience is the best remedy (or medicine).</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忍耐是最好的药物。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Patience, time, and money overcome everything.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>耐心，时间和金钱可以征服一切。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>People do not lack strength; they lack will.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人们不缺力量，缺的是决心。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Perseverance is failing nineteen times and succeeding the twentieth.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>失败十九次，坚持而不动，待到二十次，大事就成功。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Perseverance is vital to success.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不屈不挠是成功之本。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Pity is akin to love.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>怜悯近乎爱情。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Plants of learning must be watered with the rain of tears.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识的幼苗要用泪雨来浇灌。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Pleasant hours fly fast.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>欢乐的时间过得快。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Pleasing everybody is pleasing nobody.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>讨好每个人，人人不讨好。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Politeness costs nothing and gains everything.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>礼貌不费分文而可赢得一切。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poor men's words have little weight.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人微言轻。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty breeds strife.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫穷引起斗争。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is apain, but no disgrace.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫困是痛苦，但不是耻辱。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is no shame, laziness is.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫穷不害羞，懒惰才可耻。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is no sin.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫穷不是罪恶。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is not a sufficient cause of disgrace, but poverty without resolution to help oneself is a disgrace.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫穷并不可耻，穷而不争气才可耻。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is the mother of all arts.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫困乃一切艺术之源。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is the reward of idleness.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>贫穷是游手好闲的报应。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Poverty is the root of all evils.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>穷困是万恶之源。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Virtue is the only true nobility.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>唯有美德是真正高贵的。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>We hope to grow old, yet we fear old age; that is, we are willing to live, and afraid to die.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们希望长大，但怕年老；就是，愿意生，而害怕死。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where passion is high there reason is low.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>感情高涨处，理智就低落。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where the knot is loose the string slips.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>结子一松掉，绳子就滑脱。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where there is a will,, there is a way(or skill).</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有决心，就有办法。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where there is no good within, no good comes out.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>没有内心的美，就没有外在的美。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where there's reek there's heat.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>无风不起浪。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where the sun enterd, the doctor does not.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>阳光照耀处，医生就不需。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where they saw chance, we see law.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>以前他们认为是偶然的，现在我们认为是必然的。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wherever he is satisfied with what he does, he has reached his culminating point--he will progress no more.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>一个人对所做的事感到自满的，就达到了顶点，不会再前进了。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Where your will is ready, your feet are light.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>下定了决心，脚步就轻盈。决心一下，脚下生风？ </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>While (or Where) there is life there is hope.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>留得青山在，不怕没柴烧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>While the grass grows the horse (or steed) starves.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>远水救不了近火。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>While the priest climbs a post, the devil climbs ten.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>道高一尺，魔高一丈。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>While the word is in your mouth, it is your own; when 'tis once spoken, 'tis another's.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>话未出口属于己，话一出口属别人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>While we breathe, there is hope.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>只要活著，就有希望。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who answers suddenly knows little.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>答得迅速，懂得不多。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who are ready to believe are easy to deceive.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>轻信的人容易受骗。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who has never tasted bitter, knows not what is sweet.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不尝黄连苦，怎知蜂蜜甜。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who has no haste in his business mountains to him seem valleys.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>做事不急，履险如夷。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who holds the purse rules the house.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>钱可神通。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who keeps company with the wolf will learn to howl.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>近朱者赤，近墨者黑。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who knows most speaks (or says) least.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>大巧若拙。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who knows not how to dissemble knows not how to live.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>掩饰感情全不会，怎样生活必不知。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who lives by hope will die by hunger.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>靠希望而生，必因饥饿而死。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who loses liberty loses all.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>失去自由即失去一切。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who makes everything right must rise early.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>要把事事都做好，必须坚持起得早。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Whom God would ruin, he first deprives of reason.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>伤天害理，天诛地灭。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who minds his own business has no time to mind other folks.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>为人只顾自己事，就无时间关心人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Whom the gods love die young.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>好人不长寿。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Whom we love best to them we can say least.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>对我们的最爱的人，我们可说的话最少。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who serves everybody gets thanks from nobody.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人人都侍候，个个不见好。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who swims in sin shall sink in sorrow.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>在罪恶中游泳的人，必将在悲哀中沈没。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who undertakes many things at once, seldom does anything well.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>许多事情同时干，一件事也办不成。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Who will not keep a penny, shall never have many.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不积少，不会成多。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wicked men obey from fear; good men, from love.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>坏人服从出于怕，好人服从出于爱。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wickedness does not go altogether unrequited.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>恶有恶报。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wilful waste makes woeful want.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>浪费招致穷困。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wine and judgement mature with age.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>酒存放年代越久越香，判断力随年龄而增长。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wine in the bottle does not quench thirst.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>瓶中之酒不解渴。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wine is mirror of the mind.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>酒后吐真言。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom in the mind is better than money in the hand.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>手里有钱财，不如胸中有文才。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom is a good purchase though we pay dear for it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>我们为了求知识，付出高价也值得。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom is better than gold or silver.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>智慧胜过金银。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom is more to be envied than riches.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>才智比财富，令人更可羡。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom is only found in truth.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>只有在真理中才能找到智慧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wisdom is to the mind what health is to the body.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>知识之于心灵，犹如健康之于身体。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wise care begets care.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>谨慎小心会导致忧心忡忡。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wise men chanbge their mind, fools never.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>聪明人随机应变，愚蠢者固执己见。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wise men have their mouth in their heart, fools their heart in their mouth.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>智者嘴在心里，蠢人心在嘴上。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wise men learn by other men's mistakes (or harms); fools by their own.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>聪明人由别人的错误获得教训，蠢人由自己的错误获得教训。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wise men love truth, whereas fools shun it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>聪明人爱真理，蠢人背弃真理。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wit bought is better than wit taught.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不经一事，不长一智。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without a friend the world is a wilderness.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>没有朋友，世界就等于一片荒野。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without danger we cannot get beyond danger.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>没有危险就不能解除危险。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without health, life is not life, life is lifeless.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如无健康的身体，生活就不成为生活，人生也毫无生气。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without hope, the heart would break.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如无希望，心就破碎。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without respect, love cannot go far.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如不相互尊重，爱情就难发展。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Without wisdom wealth is worthless.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如果没有智慧，财富就无价值。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>With time and patience the leaf of the mulberry becomes satin.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>只要功夫深，铁杵磨成针。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wit once bought is worth twice taught.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>亲身一次的经验，抵得上老师两次的教导。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wit without learning is like a tree without fruit.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>仅有机智而无真才实学，犹如一棵大树不结果。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Wonders are many, and nothing is more wonderful than man.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>奇迹很多，但没有一件东西比人更为奇妙。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Work makes the workman.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>工作出工匠。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Work today, for you know not how much you may be hindered tomorrow.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>今天有事今天做，明天可能事受阻。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Work will not kill a man but worry will.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>累不死人愁死人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Worry kills more men than work.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>忧虑比劳累更伤人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Would you know your daughter, see her in company.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>若要知道你女儿，且看她和谁交往。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Write down the advice of him that loves you, though you like it not at present.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>爱你的忠言且记下，即使你目前不爱它。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Write it on your heart every day is the best day of the year.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>要记住，每天是一年中最好的一天。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Years bring wisdom.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>年长智也增。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Yesterday is dead, forget it; tomorrow does not exist, don't worry; today is here, use it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>昨天已经消逝，把它忘掉；明天还未来到，不必烦恼；今天就在眼前，把它用好。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Yesterday will not be called again.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>光阴一去不复返。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You are the greatest enemy if you are a coward, but if you are brave, you are your greatest friend.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>如果你是胆小鬼，你就是自己最大的敌人；如果你是勇敢者，你就是自己最好的朋友。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You can do more than strike while the iron is hot; you can make the iron hot by striking.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>铁热时，你能做的不止是锤打，而锤打可使铁热。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You can fool some of the people all the time, and all of the people some of the time; but you can't fool all of the people all the time.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>你可以一直愚弄一些人，甚至可以在某个时期愚弄所有的人；但不能一直愚弄所有的人。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You cannot clap with one hand.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>孤掌难鸣。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You cannot flay the same ox twice.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>一头牛不能剥两次皮。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>You cannot judge a tree by its bark.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>人不可貌相。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You cannot make a crab walk straight.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>江山易改，本性难移。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You cannot sell the cow and sup the milk.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>你不可能出售乳牛，同时又要喝牛奶。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You can take a horse to the water but you cannot make him drink.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>马到河边不喝水，逼马低头亦枉然。(不要逼人做他不愿做的事) </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You can't eat your cake and have it.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>不能既要吃饼，又要把饼保存。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You can't make bricks without straw.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>没有稻草，制砖难搞。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>You may force a man to shut his eyes, but you cannot make him sleep.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>你可以迫人闭眼，但不能使他睡觉。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>You (or One) cannot make a silk purse out of a sow's ear.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>粗瓷碗雕不出细花来。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>You roll my log and I'll roll yours.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>互相吹嘘。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Youth is a blunder; manhood a struggle, old age a regret.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>青年冒失莽撞；成年发奋图强；老年遗憾懊丧。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Youth is life's seed-time.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>青年时代是人生的播种期。 </center></font><br>
<center><font size=5 color=Red>Youth is the season of hope, enterprise, and energy, to a nation as well as an individual.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>青年时期对国家和个人都是希望、创业和精力充沛的时期。 </center></font><br>

<center><font size=5 color=Red>Zeal without knowledge is fire without light.</font></center><br><hr><font color=Green><center>有热情而无知识，犹如有火焰而无光芒。 </font>
